Here's a collection of mate in 3's with citation, FEN and solution.  The 
solution is 'almost unique', ie, the winner has only a single move that must 
be made to fulfill the mate.  This is suitable for creating an interactive
 puzzle where you might want to rate the puzzle and the solver.  

Bill Harvey

solution is 'almost unique', ie, the winner has only a single move that must 
be made to fulfill the mate - suitable for creating an interactive puzzle
where you might want to rate the puzzle and the solver.
